      </div>


                                      </div>
                </div>

                <p class="post-preview-excerpt">
                  The chess coaching job virtually takes up my time from 2+pm to late evenings from Mondays to Saturdays so there's hardly any chance of going to chess clubs on weekdays and even when the odd Sunday event occurs, the thought of spending a 7th day at...
                </p>
